SquidUtils uses HOCON for its configuration. To get started, create a new .conf file in this folder,
start scripting. There's an example file with the syntax and all the available options here: git.io/vwjn3.

There's a Notepad++ script for HOCON available here: coolsquid.me/files/HOCON.xml.
To install it, open Notepad++, click "Language", and choose "Define your language...".
Pick "Import", and open the XML file you just downloaded. The script has now been applied,
and should automatically appear in all .conf files.
